A couple minutes later we asked the old guy if he can put up the railings for my friend's little brother so that he can actually have some fun, but he didn't not want to do that and the reason was that he thought, "You guys are just going to be using it like it's a pinball machine and it's going to break it." <user_id>101212127826356482493<//user_id>< Name>
Charley Irvine<//Name>
<Time>1612981387164<//Time><Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Meet tea is a milk tea shop that I frequented a lot before COVID hit. It's a really nice and cozy spot for hanging out with groups of 4 or more. There's a bunch of games that you can check out and there are tables that you can put together to seat everyone. Not only that, but they serve common asian snacks like fries and popcorn chicken. This combination really just makes it outstanding for lounging and having a good time with your pals.
If you don't want to eat their food, there are other options nearby.
The parking isn't too bad either since it's also in a plaza.

The only cons that I have are that the drinks that I've had were a bit lackluster. I had the taro milk tea with boba and it feels like i'm drinking marshmallows. I tend to like my boba more firm but to each their own.<//review>

< Review>
Meet Tea is a tea boba house place on SGValley located in a huge plaza by Las Tunas ave. Interior atmosphere was chill, neat and spacious. I was in the neighborhood on a warm weekday afternoon and stumbled upon this place. I decided to check it out and they do have good selection of slush, milk teas and food. I ordered their watermelon slush and guava green tea with boba; its flavor taste good, perfectly sweetened good. Boba's texture was soft, sweet, chewy and warm. Prices were fair, affordable and competitive. Service was moderately fast. Staff was attentive and competent. They offer small, medium, large and XL cup sizes. Parking lot is huge. Overall I had a good takout experience and definitely one of the best boba tea house in the area.< /Review>

<Resp>None<//Resp><review>If you grew up in Temple City, you know Meet Tea's location used to be home to Tenju.

Small parking lot. Service was fine. Drinks came out quickly even though they said the boba cook time was 10-15 minutes.

Very similar decor and set up like how Tenju used to be. Even the menu drinks are the same, they have Monk's blend (my Tenju favorite). They have a unique fancy drinks menu, typical of most boba shops now. I wish they had descriptions under the names!

Boba Milk Tea, large - $4.99 - Milk tea was fresh and not overly sweet at 25%. Only let down was the boba. Waited 10 minutes for cold, non chewy boba. Fresh boba is warm and super soft, this definitely was not.

Batman - $4.99 - Black coffee with sweet whipped milk on top. Got 25% sweet and it was still bordering on sweet. Coffee was smooth and strong. When mixed it is a good creamy coffee.

I never understand why boba places never have a constant supply of boba ready?!?< /review>< Time>

< Text>
Upon visiting this place we noticed it's more of a restaurant than a bakery, although if you speak to the workers they can give you a selection of cakes you can order. The food was surprisingly good for the price. Because they make their food fresh, they take a little longer so i would recommend to call ahead and place your order. I tried the dumplings and teriyaki fries, way better than expected! The downside to this place is limited 2 space parking, but that's not a big enough deal to rate a 4 star. Will be returning to this place to try more freshly made food!!< /Text>
